Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 4-rules system (4 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TRFCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 8-rules system (5 strict rules).
Removing 2 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 6-rules system (3 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 87-rules system (10 strict rules).
Removing 7 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 80-rules system (10 strict rules).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 5 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 79-rules system (9 strict rules).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 5 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 78-rules system (9 strict rules).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 5 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 77-rules system (9 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 1144-rules system (31 strict rules).
Removing 93 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 1051-rules system (31 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 1048-rules system (31 strict rules).
Removing 670 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 378-rules system (0 strict rules).
